  {
    CaptionML=ENU=General Overview;
    OnPreReport=VAR
                  ReportLinesSetup@1100529600 : Record 11126218;
                BEGIN
                  ReportLinesSetup.SETRANGE("Report ID", REPORT::"General Overview");
                  IF ReportLinesSetup.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                    IF CONFIRM(Text001) THEN BEGIN
                      ReportLinesSetup.InsertDefaultLines(REPORT::"General Overview");
                      COMMIT;
                    END;
                    PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ReportLinesSetup);
                  END;

                  MaxPrognosesCount := 20;

                  GLSetup.GET;
                  NormalFormatString := Text008 + GLSetup."Amount Decimal Places" + Text009;

                  CASE RoundingFactor OF
                    RoundingFactor::None:
                      RoundingText := '';
                    RoundingFactor::"1":
                      RoundingText := Text011;
                    RoundingFactor::"1000":
                      RoundingText := Text012;
                    RoundingFactor::"1000000":
                      RoundingText := Text013;
                  END;
                END;

    PreviewMode=PrintLayout;
  }

  CODE
  {
    VAR
      Text001@1100529600 : TextConst 'ENU=Create default lines?';
      GLSetup@1100529625 : Record 98;
      TmpPrognosisDates@1100529602 : TEMPORARY Record 2000000007;
      TmpPrognosisChartData@1100529604 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;
      TmpReportLineData@1100529601 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;
      TmpReportTotalLine@1100529611 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;
      TmpReportSubTotalLine@1100529618 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;
      TmpPrognosisLinePurch@1100529607 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;
      TmpCostObjectContract@1100529629 : TEMPORARY Record 349;
      CostControlMgt@1100529605 : Codeunit 11012006;
      ShowBuyersOptions@1100529615 : Boolean;
      PrognosisDateArray@1100529603 : ARRAY [5] OF Date;
      FilterDate@1100529613 : Date;
      PrognosisDate@1100529606 : Date;
      ProjectNo@1100529617 : Code[20];
      EstimateResult@1100529609 : Decimal;
      EstimateResultExt@1100529608 : Decimal;
      EstimateResultOpt@1100529612 : Decimal;
      PrognosesCount@1100529614 : Integer;
      MaxPrognosesCount@1100529616 : Integer;
      StartPageNo@1100527700 : Integer;
      RoundingFactor@1100529619 : 'None,1,1000,1000000';
      CostObjectFilter@1100529610 : Text;
      RoundingText@1100529621 : Text[80];
      NormalFormatString@1100529620 : Text[80];
      Text008@1100529624 : TextConst 'ENU=<Precision,;NOR=<Precision,;SVE=<Precision,';
      Text009@1100529623 : TextConst 'ENU=><Standard Format,0>;NOR=><Standard Format,0>;SVE=><Standard Format,0>';
      Text010@1100529622 : TextConst 'ENU=<Precision,1><Standard Format,0>;NOR=<Precision,1><Standard Format,0>;SVE=<Precision,1><Standard Format,0>';
      Text011@1100529628 : TextConst 'ENU=Amounts are rounded to 1;NOR=Bel›p er rundet av til 1;SVE=Belopp avrundas till 1';
      Text012@1100529627 : TextConst 'ENU=Amounts are in whole 1000s.;NOR=Bel›pene er i hele 1000.;SVE=Belopp „r i hela 1000-tal.';
      Text013@1100529626 : TextConst 'ENU=Amounts are in whole 1000000s.;NOR=Bel›pene er i hele 1000000.;SVE=Belopp „r i hela 1000000-tal.';

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetReportName@1100525003() : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(DELSTR(CurrReport.OBJECTID, 1, STRPOS(CurrReport.OBJECTID, ' ')));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetReportFilter@1100525000() : Text;
    VAR
      ProjectFilter0@1100529601 : Text;
      ProjectFilter2@1100529600 : Text;
    BEGIN
      ProjectFilter0 := Project.GETFILTERS;
      Project.FILTERGROUP(2);
      ProjectFilter2 := Project.GETFILTERS;
      Project.FILTERGROUP(0);

      IF (ProjectFilter0 = '') AND (ProjectFilter2 = '') THEN
        EXIT;

      IF ProjectFilter2 <> '' THEN
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2, %3', Project.TABLECAPTION, ProjectFilter0, ProjectFilter2))
      ELSE
        EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('%1: %2', Project.TABLECAPTION, ProjectFilter0));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetPrognosisDate@1100529602();
    VAR
      Prognosis@1100529600 : Record 11012034;
    BEGIN
      PrognosisDate := FilterDate;
      TmpPrognosisDates.DELETEALL;
      PrognosesCount := 0;

      Prognosis.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      Prognosis.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", 0D, FilterDate);
      Prognosis.SETRANGE("Select For Reporting", TRUE);
      IF Prognosis.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT;

      Prognosis.FINDLAST;
      PrognosisDate := Prognosis."Prognosis Date";
      REPEAT
        TmpPrognosisDates."Period Start" := Prognosis."Prognosis Date";
        TmpPrognosisDates.INSERT;
        PrognosesCount += 1;
      UNTIL (Prognosis.NEXT(-1) = 0) OR (PrognosesCount = MaxPrognosesCount);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetPrognosisChartData@1100529600();
    VAR
      PrognosisLine@1100529603 : Record 11012035;
      PrognosisMgt@1100529600 : Codeunit 11020217;
      i@1100529604 : Integer;
      CostType@1100529602 : ' ,Labor,Material,Subcontracting,Plant,Sundry,Revenues';
      CostObjectFilter@1100529601 : Text;
      EstimateResultLoc@1100529605 : Decimal;
      DivBy@1100529606 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TmpPrognosisChartData.DELETEALL;
      CLEAR(PrognosisDateArray);
      IF PrognosesCount = 0 THEN
        EXIT;

      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      PrognosisMgt.CalcEstimateResultPrognosis(Project."No.", PrognosisDate, CostType, CostObjectFilter,
        TmpReportLineData.Dec1, TmpReportLineData.Dec2, TmpReportLineData.Dec3, TmpReportLineData.Dec4);
      IF CostObjectFilter <> '' THEN
        EstimateResultLoc := TmpReportLineData.Dec1 + TmpReportLineData.Dec2 + TmpReportLineData.Dec3 + TmpReportLineData.Dec4
      ELSE
        EstimateResultLoc := EstimateResult + EstimateResultExt + EstimateResultOpt;

      CLEAR(TmpReportLineData);

      CASE RoundingFactor OF
        RoundingFactor::None,
        RoundingFactor::"1":
          DivBy := 1;
        RoundingFactor::"1000":
          DivBy := 1000;
        RoundingFactor::"1000000":
          DivBy := 1000000;
      END;

      i := PrognosesCount;
      TmpPrognosisDates.FINDSET;
      REPEAT
        TmpPrognosisChartData.INIT;
        TmpPrognosisChartData."Key Code1" := FORMAT(i);
        TmpPrognosisChartData.Date1 := TmpPrognosisDates."Period Start";
        TmpPrognosisChartData.Dec1 := EstimateResultLoc / DivBy;

        PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", TmpPrognosisDates."Period Start");
        PrognosisLine.CALCSUMS("Prognosis End Result");
        TmpPrognosisChartData.Dec2 := PrognosisLine."Prognosis End Result" / DivBy;

        TmpPrognosisChartData.INSERT;

        IF i <= 5 THEN
          PrognosisDateArray[i] := TmpPrognosisDates."Period Start";
        i -= 1;
      UNTIL TmpPrognosisDates.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetReportLineData@1100529608();
    VAR
      ReportLinesSetup@1100529600 : Record 11126218;
      CodeLoc@1100529601 : Code[10];
    BEGIN
      TmpReportLineData.RESET;
      TmpReportLineData.DELETEALL;

      TmpReportTotalLine.DELETEALL;
      TmpReportTotalLine.INIT;
      TmpReportTotalLine.INSERT;

      TmpReportSubTotalLine.DELETEALL;
      TmpReportSubTotalLine.INIT;
      TmpReportSubTotalLine.INSERT;

      TmpPrognosisLinePurch.RESET;
      TmpPrognosisLinePurch.DELETEALL;

      GetCostObjectContractList;
      CodeLoc := '000';

      ReportLinesSetup.SETRANGE("Report ID", REPORT::"General Overview");
      IF ReportLinesSetup.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          CodeLoc := INCSTR(CodeLoc);
          TmpReportLineData.INIT;
          TmpReportLineData."Key Code1" := CodeLoc;
          TmpReportLineData.Text1 := ReportLinesSetup."Line Caption";
          TmpReportLineData.Bool1 := ReportLinesSetup.Bold;
          TmpReportLineData.Int1 := ReportLinesSetup."Line Type";
          TmpReportLineData.INSERT;

          CASE ReportLinesSetup."Line Type" OF
            ReportLinesSetup."Line Type"::Caption:
              BEGIN
                TmpReportSubTotalLine.DELETEALL;
                TmpReportSubTotalLine.INIT;
                TmpReportSubTotalLine.INSERT;
              END;

            ReportLinesSetup."Line Type"::Data:
              BEGIN
                CostObjectFilter := ReportLinesSetup.GetCostObjectFilter(ReportLinesSetup."Cost Group Code", ReportLinesSetup."Cost Type");

                IF ReportLinesSetup."Estimate Result" THEN
                  CreateEstimateReportLine(ReportLinesSetup)
                ELSE
                  CreateReportLine(ReportLinesSetup);

                CalcPercentageOfCompletion(TmpReportLineData);
                TmpReportLineData.MODIFY;

                UpdateTmpReportLine(TmpReportSubTotalLine, TmpReportLineData, FALSE);
                UpdateTmpReportLine(TmpReportTotalLine, TmpReportLineData, FALSE);
              END;

            ReportLinesSetup."Line Type"::Contract:
              BEGIN
                TmpReportLineData.Dec1 := Project."Contract Amount";
                TmpReportLineData.Dec2 := Project."Extension Contract Amount";
                TmpReportLineData.Dec3 := Project."Options Contract Amount";
                TmpReportLineData.Dec5 := TmpReportLineData.Dec1 + TmpReportLineData.Dec2 + TmpReportLineData.Dec3;
                TmpReportLineData.MODIFY;
              END;

            ReportLinesSetup."Line Type"::Subtotal:
              BEGIN
                UpdateTmpReportLine(TmpReportLineData, TmpReportSubTotalLine, TRUE);
                TmpReportSubTotalLine.DELETEALL;
                TmpReportSubTotalLine.INIT;
                TmpReportSubTotalLine.INSERT;
              END;
          END;
        UNTIL ReportLinesSetup.NEXT = 0;

      CalcPercentageOfCompletion(TmpReportTotalLine);
      TmpReportTotalLine.MODIFY;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateReportLine@1100529610(ReportLinesSetup@1100529602 : Record 11126218);
    VAR
      ProjectResultForecast@1100529603 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      GetTmpPrognosisLine(ReportLinesSetup, PrognosisDate);
      IF ReportLinesSetup."Values Inside Purch. Contr." THEN BEGIN
        TmpReportLineData.Dec1 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec1;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec2 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec2;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec3 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec3;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec4 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec4;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec5 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec5;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec6 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec6;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TmpReportLineData.Dec1 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec10;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec2 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec11;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec3 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec12;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec4 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec13;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec5 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec14;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec6 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec15;
      END;

      IF TmpPrognosisChartData.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          GetTmpPrognosisLine(ReportLinesSetup, TmpPrognosisChartData.Date1);
          IF ReportLinesSetup."Values Inside Purch. Contr." THEN
            ProjectResultForecast := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec7
          ELSE
            ProjectResultForecast := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec16;
          CASE TmpPrognosisChartData."Key Code1" OF
            '1': TmpReportLineData.Dec11 := ProjectResultForecast;
            '2': TmpReportLineData.Dec12 := ProjectResultForecast;
            '3': TmpReportLineData.Dec13 := ProjectResultForecast;
            '4': TmpReportLineData.Dec14 := ProjectResultForecast;
            '5': TmpReportLineData.Dec15 := ProjectResultForecast;
          END;
        UNTIL TmpPrognosisChartData.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateEstimateReportLine@1100529606(ReportLinesSetup@1100529601 : Record 11126218);
    VAR
      TotalEstimateResultLoc@1100529600 : Decimal;
      GetResultFromPrognosis@1100529602 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      GetResultFromPrognosis := (ReportLinesSetup."Cost Type" <> 0) OR (CostObjectFilter <> '');

      IF GetResultFromPrognosis THEN BEGIN
        GetTmpPrognosisLine(ReportLinesSetup, PrognosisDate);
        TmpReportLineData.Dec1 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec1 + TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec10;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec2 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec2 + TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec11;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec3 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec3 + TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec12;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec4 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec4 + TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec13;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec5 := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec5 + TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec14;
      END;

      IF (TmpReportLineData.Dec1 = 0) AND (TmpReportLineData.Dec2 = 0) AND (TmpReportLineData.Dec3 = 0) AND (TmpReportLineData.Dec4 = 0) THEN BEGIN
        TmpReportLineData.Dec1 := EstimateResult;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec2 := EstimateResultExt;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec3 := EstimateResultOpt;
        TmpReportLineData.Dec5 := TmpReportLineData.Dec1 + TmpReportLineData.Dec2 + TmpReportLineData.Dec3;
      END;

      IF TmpPrognosisChartData.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          IF GetResultFromPrognosis THEN BEGIN
            GetTmpPrognosisLine(ReportLinesSetup, TmpPrognosisChartData.Date1);
            TotalEstimateResultLoc := TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec7 + TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec16;
          END ELSE
            TotalEstimateResultLoc := CostControlMgt.CalcTotalEstimateResult(Project."No.", TmpPrognosisChartData.Date1);
          CASE TmpPrognosisChartData."Key Code1" OF
            '1': TmpReportLineData.Dec11 := TotalEstimateResultLoc;
            '2': TmpReportLineData.Dec12 := TotalEstimateResultLoc;
            '3': TmpReportLineData.Dec13 := TotalEstimateResultLoc;
            '4': TmpReportLineData.Dec14 := TotalEstimateResultLoc;
            '5': TmpReportLineData.Dec15 := TotalEstimateResultLoc;
          END;
        UNTIL TmpPrognosisChartData.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateTmpReportLine@1100529614(VAR LocTmpReportLine@1100529600 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;SourceReportLine@1100529601 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579;UpdatePerc@1100529602 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec1 += SourceReportLine.Dec1;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec2 += SourceReportLine.Dec2;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec3 += SourceReportLine.Dec3;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec4 += SourceReportLine.Dec4;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec5 += SourceReportLine.Dec5;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec6 += SourceReportLine.Dec6;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec11 += SourceReportLine.Dec11;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec12 += SourceReportLine.Dec12;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec13 += SourceReportLine.Dec13;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec14 += SourceReportLine.Dec14;
      LocTmpReportLine.Dec15 += SourceReportLine.Dec15;
      IF UpdatePerc THEN
        CalcPercentageOfCompletion(LocTmpReportLine);
      LocTmpReportLine.MODIFY;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetTmpPrognosisLine@1100529612(ReportLinesSetup@1100529602 : Record 11126218;PrognosisDateLoc@1100529600 : Date);
    VAR
      TmpPrognosisLine1@1100529603 : TEMPORARY Record 11012035;
      TmpPrognosisLine2@1100529604 : TEMPORARY Record 11012035;
    BEGIN
      TmpPrognosisLinePurch.SETRANGE("Key Code1", FORMAT(ReportLinesSetup."Line No."));
      TmpPrognosisLinePurch.SETRANGE(Date1, PrognosisDateLoc);
      IF NOT TmpPrognosisLinePurch.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.INIT;
        SplitPurchasePrognosisAmount(ProjectNo, PrognosisDateLoc,
          ReportLinesSetup."Cost Type", CostObjectFilter,
          TmpPrognosisLine1, TmpPrognosisLine2);

        TmpPrognosisLinePurch."Key Code1" := FORMAT(ReportLinesSetup."Line No.");
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch."Key Code2" := FORMAT(DATE2DMY(PrognosisDateLoc, 1));
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch."Key Code3" := FORMAT(DATE2DMY(PrognosisDateLoc, 2));
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch."Key Code4" := FORMAT(DATE2DMY(PrognosisDateLoc, 3));
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Date1 := PrognosisDateLoc;

        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec1 := TmpPrognosisLine1."Original Budget Amount";
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec2 := TmpPrognosisLine1.Extension;
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec3 := TmpPrognosisLine1.Options;
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec4 := TmpPrognosisLine1.Adjustments;
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec5 := TmpPrognosisLine1."Budget Amount";
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec6 := TmpPrognosisLine1."Actual Costs";
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec7 := TmpPrognosisLine1."Prognosis End Result";

        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec10 := TmpPrognosisLine2."Original Budget Amount";
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec11 := TmpPrognosisLine2.Extension;
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec12 := TmpPrognosisLine2.Options;
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec13 := TmpPrognosisLine2.Adjustments;
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec14 := TmpPrognosisLine2."Budget Amount";
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec15 := TmpPrognosisLine2."Actual Costs";
        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.Dec16 := TmpPrognosisLine2."Prognosis End Result";

        TmpPrognosisLinePurch.INSERT;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SplitPurchasePrognosisAmount@1100529603(ProjectNo@1100529611 : Code[20];PrognosisDate@1100529608 : Date;CostType@1100529600 : Integer;CostObjectFilter@1100529607 : Text;VAR TmpPrognosisLine1@1100529604 : TEMPORARY Record 11012035;VAR TmpPrognosisLine2@1100529603 : TEMPORARY Record 11012035);
    VAR
      Prognosis@1100529601 : Record 11012034;
      PrognosisLine@1100529610 : Record 11012035;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(TmpPrognosisLine1);
      CLEAR(TmpPrognosisLine2);

      IF NOT Prognosis.GET(ProjectNo, PrognosisDate) THEN
        EXIT;
      IF NOT Prognosis."Select For Reporting" THEN
        EXIT;

      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Project No.", ProjectNo);
      PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date", PrognosisDate);
      IF CostType > 0 THEN
        PrognosisLine.SETRANGE("Cost Type", CostType - 1);
      IF CostObjectFilter <> '' THEN
        PrognosisLine.SETFILTER("Cost Object", CostObjectFilter);
      IF PrognosisLine.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT;

      PrognosisLine.FINDSET;
      REPEAT
        IF CostObjectIsContract(PrognosisLine."Cost Object") THEN BEGIN
          TmpPrognosisLine1."Budget Amount" += PrognosisLine."Budget Amount";
          TmpPrognosisLine1."Original Budget Amount" += PrognosisLine."Original Budget Amount";
          TmpPrognosisLine1.Options += PrognosisLine.Options;
          TmpPrognosisLine1.Extension += PrognosisLine.Extension;
          TmpPrognosisLine1.Adjustments += PrognosisLine.Adjustments;
          TmpPrognosisLine1."Actual Costs" += PrognosisLine."Actual Costs";
          TmpPrognosisLine1."Prognosis End Result" += PrognosisLine."Prognosis End Result";
        END ELSE BEGIN
          TmpPrognosisLine2."Budget Amount" += PrognosisLine."Budget Amount";
          TmpPrognosisLine2."Original Budget Amount" += PrognosisLine."Original Budget Amount";
          TmpPrognosisLine2.Options += PrognosisLine.Options;
          TmpPrognosisLine2.Extension += PrognosisLine.Extension;
          TmpPrognosisLine2.Adjustments += PrognosisLine.Adjustments;
          TmpPrognosisLine2."Actual Costs" += PrognosisLine."Actual Costs";
          TmpPrognosisLine2."Prognosis End Result" += PrognosisLine."Prognosis End Result";
        END;
      UNTIL PrognosisLine.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetCostObjectContractList@1100529607();
    VAR
      LocProjectPurchaseAction@1100529602 : Record 11012026;
    BEGIN
      TmpCostObjectContract.RESET;
      TmpCostObjectContract.DELETEALL;

      LocProjectPurchaseAction.SETRANGE("Project No.", Project."No.");
      LocProjectPurchaseAction.SETFILTER("Default Cost Object Purchase", '<>%1', '');
      IF LocProjectPurchaseAction.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT;

      LocProjectPurchaseAction.FINDSET;
      REPEAT
        TmpCostObjectContract.SETRANGE(Code, LocProjectPurchaseAction."Default Cost Object Purchase");
        IF TmpCostObjectContract.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
          TmpCostObjectContract.Code := LocProjectPurchaseAction."Default Cost Object Purchase";
          TmpCostObjectContract.INSERT;
        END;
      UNTIL LocProjectPurchaseAction.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CostObjectIsContract@1100529605(CostObjectCode@1100529600 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      TmpCostObjectContract.SETRANGE(Code, CostObjectCode);
      EXIT(NOT TmpCostObjectContract.ISEMPTY);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetFilterDate@1100529604();
    VAR
      Prognosis@1100529600 : Record 11012034;
    BEGIN
      IF ProjectNo = '' THEN BEGIN
        FilterDate := 0D;
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF NOT Prognosis.GET(ProjectNo, FilterDate) THEN
        FilterDate := 0D
      ELSE
        IF NOT Prognosis."Select For Reporting" THEN
          FilterDate := 0D;

      IF FilterDate = 0D THEN BEGIN
        Prognosis.SETRANGE("Project No.", ProjectNo);
        Prognosis.SETRANGE("Select For Reporting", TRUE);
        IF Prognosis.FINDLAST THEN
          FilterDate := Prognosis."Prognosis Date";
        EXIT;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE RoundAmount@1100529634(Value@1102 : Decimal) : Text;
    BEGIN
      CASE RoundingFactor OF
        RoundingFactor::None:
          EXIT(FORMAT(Value, 0, NormalFormatString));
        RoundingFactor::"1":
          EXIT(FORMAT((ROUND(Value, 1))));
        RoundingFactor::"1000":
          EXIT(FORMAT(ROUND(Value / 1000, 0.1), 0, Text010));
        RoundingFactor::"1000000":
          EXIT(FORMAT(ROUND(Value / 1000000, 0.1), 0, Text010));
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CalcPercentageOfCompletion@1100529611(VAR LocTmpReportLine@1100529600 : TEMPORARY Record 11020579);
    BEGIN
      IF LocTmpReportLine.Dec5 - LocTmpReportLine.Dec11 = 0 THEN
        LocTmpReportLine.Dec7 := 0
      ELSE
        LocTmpReportLine.Dec7 := LocTmpReportLine.Dec6 / (LocTmpReportLine.Dec5 - LocTmpReportLine.Dec11);
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE SetCommonParameters@1100529601(NewProjectNo@1100529600 : Code[20];NewFilterDate@1100529601 : Date;NewStartPageNo@1100527701 : Integer;NewRoundingFactor@1100529603 : 'None,1,1000,1000000');
    BEGIN
      ProjectNo := NewProjectNo;
      FilterDate := NewFilterDate;
      StartPageNo := NewStartPageNo;
      RoundingFactor := NewRoundingFactor;
    END;

    [External]
    PROCEDURE SetSpecificParameters@1100527700(NewShowBuyersOptions@1100529602 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      ShowBuyersOptions := NewShowBuyersOptions;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Shared TotalPrinted As Boolean

Public Function LastRowIsTotal(ByVal Value As Boolean) As Boolean
    If TotalPrinted = False Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return False
    End If
    If TotalPrinted = True Then
        TotalPrinted = Value
        Return True
    End If
End Function

Shared Data as Object

Public Function SetData(NewData as Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data = NewData
    End If
End Function

Public Function GetData(Num as Integer) as Object
  Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data),Chr(177))))
End Function
